}require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'qualtrics_survey','handlers',['handlers']);
/** Private javascript for qualtrics survey placement
 * We want to show on the 2nd pageview, no more than once every 30 days
 * The div id is generated from the qualtrics site-intercept code.
 * The placement render will decide which survey to displace.
 */
define([
    "placement",
    "lib/jquery-amd",
    "ta",
    'ta/Core/TA.LocalStorage',
    'ta/Core/TA.Event',
    'page-model',
    'ta/util/RecordInterruption',
    'ta/support/Qualtrics',
    'utils/throttle'
  ],
  function (placement, $, ta, taLocalStore, taEvent, model, recordInterruption, taQualtrics, throttle) {
    "use strict";

    ta.queueForLoad(function () {
      // For surveys that should hide when the user begins to scroll, this is the how much give they have
      var SCROLL_BUFFER = 318;
      // Campaign ID for event tracking
      var CAMPAIGN_ID = 'qualtrics_surveys';
      var placementEl = $('#' + placement.id);

      taQualtrics.setSmartSurvey(!!placement.params.smartSurvey);

      taQualtrics.updatePageViews();

      if (taLocalStore.enabled && ( taQualtrics.canDisplaySmart() || ( !taQualtrics.getSmartSurvey() && taQualtrics.canDisplay() ) )) {
        var surveyKey = placementEl.find(".survey_plc_holder").attr('id');
        var surveyContainerClassName = '.' + surveyKey + '_InfoBarContainer';
        var surveyName = placementEl.find(".survey_name").attr('id');
        var surveyProperties = 'Qualtrics_Survey' + '|' + window.pageServlet + '|' + surveyName;

        if (placement.params.smartSurvey) {
          var getSurveyProperties = function (_ss, _qa) {
            return _ss + '|' + ['sc-' + _qa.getSessionCount(), 'ir-' + _qa.getInterceptReqs(), 'iv-' + _qa.getInterceptViews(), 'pv-'+_qa.getPageViews()].join('|');
          };
          ta.on('qxInterceptShown', function () {
            ta.trackEventOnPage(CAMPAIGN_ID, 'interceptShown', getSurveyProperties(surveyProperties, taQualtrics), null, true);

            taQualtrics.updateInterceptViews();
            taQualtrics.updateSessionCount();
          });

          ta.on('qxInterceptAccept', function () {
            ta.trackEventOnPage(CAMPAIGN_ID, 'interceptAccept', getSurveyProperties(surveyProperties, taQualtrics), null, false);

            taQualtrics.setResponded(true);
          });

          ta.on('qxInterceptDecline', function () {
            ta.trackEventOnPage(CAMPAIGN_ID, 'interceptDecline', getSurveyProperties(surveyProperties, taQualtrics), null, false);

            taQualtrics.setResponded(true);
          });
        }

        if (surveyKey) {
          taQualtrics.displaySurvey(surveyKey);
          recordInterruption.record('popup', surveyProperties, taQualtrics.getPageViews());

          if (placement.params.smartSurvey) {
            taQualtrics.updateInterceptReqs();
          }

          // TV-1243 - Mobile Surveys cover a commerce component, so they should be hidden when the user begins to scroll
          if (placement.params.hideOnScroll) {
            var hide = function () {
              var scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop;
              if (scrollTop > SCROLL_BUFFER) {
                $(surveyContainerClassName).hide();
              }
            };
            $(window).on('scroll', throttle(hide, 100));
          }
        }
      }
    });

    return {
    };
  });
});require(['ta/prwidgets'], function(widgets) {
var define = widgets.define.bind(widgets,'search_typeahead','dt_overlay',['dt_overlay','handlers']);
/* jshint newcap:false */
define(['api-mod', 'lib/jquery-amd'],
       function (api, $) {

    'use strict';

    var iconFontMap = {
        ALL: 'ui_icon globe-world',
        GEO: 'ui_icon map-pin-fill',
        HOTELOVERVIEW: 'ui_icon map-pin-fill',
        HOTEL: 'ui_icon hotels',
        ATTRACTION: 'ui_icon attractions',
        EATERY: 'ui_icon restaurants',
        VACATION_RENTAL: 'ui_icon vacation-rentals',
        FLIGHTS_TO: "ui_icon flights",
        AIRPORT: "ui_icon flights",
        THEME_PARK: "ui_icon amusement-parks",
        VACATION_PACKAGE: "ui_icon hotels",
        SMART_DEAL: 'ui_icon hotels',
        CHILD_TOP: 'sprite-typeahead-connector-top',
        CHILD_BOTTOM: 'sprite-typeahead-connector-bottom',
        NEIGHBORHOOD: 'ui_icon neighborhoods',
        TRAVEL_GUIDE: 'ui_icon guides',
        AIRLINE: 'ui_icon flights',
        ACTIVITY: 'ui_icon activities',
        NEARBY: 'ui_icon nearby-fill',
        SEARCH: 'ui_icon',
        NEAR_POI: 'ui_icon map-pin-fill'
    };

    var isRtl = api.hasClass(document.body, 'rtl');

    var createResultElements = function (results, query) {
        var resultElements = [];
        if (results && results.length) {
            var totalResults = 0;
            var length = results.length;
            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                var result = results[i];
                var node;
                if (result.sectionTitle) {
                    node = titleTemplate(result.sectionTitle);
                } else {
                    node = itemTemplate(result);
                    totalResults += 1;
                }
                node.resultIdx = i;
                result.resultIdx = i;
                result.query = query;
                result.totalCount = totalResults;
                resultElements.push(node);
            }
        }
        return resultElements;
    };

    var getIcon = function (item) {
        var itemClass = '';
        if (item.type) {
            if (item.isNeighborhood) {
                itemClass = iconFontMap.NEIGHBORHOOD;
            } else if (item.data_type == 'NEAR_POI') {
                itemClass = iconFontMap.NEAR_POI;
            } else {
                var itemType = item.type.toUpperCase();
                itemClass = iconFontMap[itemType] || item.type;
            }
        } else if (item.navi) {
          itemClass = (item.resultIdx == 0) ? 'ui_icon single-chevron-left' : 'ui_icon single-chevron-right';
        }
        return api.createElement('div', {'class': itemClass});
    };

    var createItemElement = function (item) {
        var itemWrapClass = 'item_wrap';
        if (item.geonavi){
          itemWrapClass += ' geonavi';
        }
        var itemWrap = api.createElement('div', {'class': itemWrapClass});
        var itemIcon = getIcon(item);
        !item.geonavi && itemWrap.appendChild(itemIcon);

        var itemContentClass = 'item_content';
        var itemContent =  api.createElement('div', {'class': itemContentClass});
        var primaryElementClass = 'primary';

        if (item.details) {
            if (item.data_type == 'NEAR_POI' && item.find_near_name) {
                primaryElementClass = primaryElementClass + ' near_poi';
            }
            var primaryElement = api.createElement('span', {'class': primaryElementClass});

            var name = item.details.name || item.name;
            var geo_name = item.details.geo_name || '';
            var nameElement = api.createElement('span', {'class': 'name'});

            if (item.data_type == 'NEAR_POI' && item.find_near_name) {
              $(nameElement).html(item.find_near_name);
            } else {
              $(nameElement).text(name);
            }

            primaryElement.appendChild(nameElement);
            itemContent.appendChild(primaryElement);
            if (geo_name) {
                var geoNameElement = api.createElement('span', {'class': 'secondary'});
                $(geoNameElement).text(geo_name);
                itemContent.appendChild(geoNameElement);
            }
        } else if (item.name) {
            if (item.data_type == 'SEARCH') {
                primaryElementClass = primaryElementClass + ' search';
            }
            primaryElement = api.createElement('span', {'class': primaryElementClass});

            if (item.data_type == 'SEARCH') {
                $(primaryElement).html(item.name);
            } else {
                $(primaryElement).text(item.name);
            }
            itemContent.appendChild(primaryElement);
        }

        itemWrap.appendChild(itemContent);
        item.geonavi && itemWrap.appendChild(itemIcon);

        return itemWrap;
    };

    var itemTemplate = function (item) {
        var itemClass = 'item';
        if (item.short) {
            itemClass = itemClass + ' short'
        }
        if (item.type && item.type == 'SEARCH') {
            itemClass = itemClass + ' query-rescue'
        }
        item.selected && (itemClass += ' selected');
        var listItem = api.createElement('li', {'class': itemClass});
        var itemElement = createItemElement(item);
        if (itemElement) {
            listItem.appendChild(itemElement);
        }
        return listItem;
    };

    var titleTemplate = function (item) {
        var listItem = api.createElement('li', {'class': 'title'});
        $(listItem).text(item);
        return listItem;
    };

    var listTemplate = function (items) {
        var listElement = api.createElement('ul');
        if (items && items.length) {
            var length = items.length;
            for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                listElement.appendChild(items[i]);
            }
        }
        return listElement;
    };

    var dtPosition = function () {
        var topOffset = 6;
        var leftOffset = isRtl ? 0 : 25;
        var widthOffset = -25;
        return function () {
            function positionOverlay() {
                /* jshint validthis:true */
                var alignElement = this.sourceElement;
                var sourceSize = api.getSize(alignElement);
                var sourcePosition = api.getPosition(alignElement);
                var windowSize = api.getSize(window);
                var isNarrowScreen = windowSize.x <= 767;
                var currentLeftOffset = isNarrowScreen ? 0 : leftOffset;
                var currentTopOffset = isNarrowScreen ? 0 : topOffset;
                var currentWidthOffset = isNarrowScreen ? 0 : widthOffset;

                // auto shrink & expand overlay width for find/near feature based on the input length
                // when auto expand/shrink overlay, we want to fix one side of the overlay depending on if rtl is true
                var leftFixedAlignment = 'left:' + (sourcePosition.left + currentLeftOffset) + 'px;';
                var rightFixedAlignment = 'right:' + (window.innerWidth - (sourcePosition.left + currentWidthOffset + sourceSize.x)) + 'px;';
                var horizontalFixedAlignment = isRtl ? rightFixedAlignment : leftFixedAlignment;
                var horizontalVariableAlignment = isRtl? 'left:auto;' : 'right:auto;';

                this.container.style.cssText =
                    'position:absolute;' +
                    horizontalFixedAlignment +
                    horizontalVariableAlignment +
                    'top:' + (sourcePosition.top + sourceSize.y + currentTopOffset) + 'px;' +
                    'min-width:' + (sourceSize.x + currentWidthOffset) + 'px;' +
                    'max-width:' + '600px;';
            }

            this.on('show', positionOverlay);
            this.on('positionDirty', positionOverlay);
            this.reposition = positionOverlay.bind(this);
        };
    };

    var mwPosition = function () {
        return function () {
            function positionOverlay() {
                this.container.style.cssText =
                  'position:fixed;' +
                  'right:0;' +
                  'left:0;' +
                  'top:0;' +
                  'bottom:0;'
            }
            this.on('show', positionOverlay);
        };
    };



    return {createResultElements: createResultElements,
            listTemplate: listTemplate,
            dtPosition: dtPosition,
            mwPosition: mwPosition};

});
});
define('utils/string/InputLength', [], function(){
'use strict';
return function(input){
var len = 0;
for (var i = input.length - 1; i >= 0; i--){
len++;
var c = input.charCodeAt(i);
if ((c >= 0x4E00 && c <= 0x9FFF) ||
(c >= 0x3040 && c <= 0x30FF) ||
(c >= 0xAC00 && c <= 0xD7FF)){
len++;
}
}
return len;
};
});

define('typeahead/TypeAhead', [
'Logging',
'api-mod',
'mixins/mixin', 'mixins/Events',
'utils/string/InputLength',
'lib/jquery-amd',
'page-model'
],
function(
Logging,
api,
mixin, Events,
inputLength,
$,
pageModel
){
'use strict';
var KEY_BKSPC = 8
, KEY_TAB = 9
, KEY_ENTER = 13
, KEY_CAPSLK = 20
, KEY_ESCAPE = 27
, KEY_LEFT = 37
, KEY_UP = 38
, KEY_RIGHT = 39
, KEY_DOWN = 40
, KEY_DELETE = 46
, KEY_META = 91
, KEY_SHIFT = 16
, KEY_CTRL = 17
;
var DEFAULT_OPTIONS = {
minChars: 3,
searchDelay: 250,
jpFfInterval: 500
};
var TypeAhead = function(options, mixins){
mixin(this, Events.create(Array.prototype.concat(TypeAhead.inputEvents, TypeAhead.emitEvents)));
this.options = $.extend({}, DEFAULT_OPTIONS, options);
this.resultElements = null;
this.selectedIndex = -1;
mixins && Array.isArray(mixins) || (mixins = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 1));
for (var i = 0; i < mixins.length; i++){
mixins[i] && mixins[i].call(this);
}
TypeAhead.inputEvents.forEach(function(type){
if (typeof this[type] == 'function'){ this.on(type, this[type]); }
}, this);
};
TypeAhead.emitEvents = ['emptyInput', 'insufficientInput', 'search', 'results',
'changeSelection', 'updateSelection', 'escape', 'enter', 'tab', 'selected',
'resultHover', 'resultUnhover', 'resultClick', 'show', 'hide', 'searchResults',
'inputChanged'];
TypeAhead.inputEvents = ['focus', 'blur', 'keydown', 'keyup', 'compositionend'];
TypeAhead.prototype.keydown = function(evt, elt){
if (!elt){ return; }
switch (evt.keyCode){
case KEY_ENTER:
api.stopEvent(evt);
this.emit('enter', elt);
break;
case KEY_DOWN:
api.stopEvent(evt);
this.emit('changeSelection', elt, 1);
break;
case KEY_UP:
api.stopEvent(evt);
this.emit('changeSelection', elt, -1);
break;
case KEY_ESCAPE:
api.stopEvent(evt);
this.emit('escape', elt);
break;
case KEY_TAB:
this.emit('tab', elt);
break;
}
};
TypeAhead.prototype.compositionend = function(evt, elt){
if (!elt){ return; }
api.stopEvent(evt);
this.emit('inputChanged', elt);
this.runSearch(elt);
};
TypeAhead.prototype.keyup = function(evt, elt){
if (!elt || this.composing){ return; }
if (evt.keyCode === KEY_ENTER) {
return;
}
clearTimeout(this.searchTimer);
switch (evt.keyCode){
case KEY_DOWN:
case KEY_UP:
case KEY_ESCAPE:
case KEY_TAB:
case KEY_CAPSLK:
case KEY_LEFT:
case KEY_RIGHT:
case KEY_META:
case KEY_SHIFT:
case KEY_CTRL:
return;
}
var self = this;
this.emit('inputChanged', elt);
this.searchTimer = setTimeout(function(){
self.runSearch(elt);
}, this.options.searchDelay);
};
if (pageModel.session.jpFfIME) {
TypeAhead.prototype.keyupAction = function(evt, elt){
if (!elt){
return;
}
clearTimeout(this.searchTimer);
var self = this;
this.searchTimer = setTimeout(function(){
self.runSearch(elt);
}, this.options.searchDelay);
};
TypeAhead.prototype.focus = function (evt, el) {
if (document.activeElement == el) {
var imeLoop = function () {
this.keyupAction.call(this, evt, el);
this.imeTimer && clearTimeout(this.imeTimer);
this.imeTimer = setTimeout(imeLoop.bind(this), this.options.jpFfInterval);
};
imeLoop.call(this);
}
};
}
TypeAhead.prototype.runSearch = function(elt){
if(this.lastQuery && this.lastQuery == elt.value){
return;
}
if (/^\s*$/.test(elt.value)){
this.emptyInput = true;
this.insufficientInput = false;
this.emit('emptyInput', elt);
} else if (inputLength(elt.value) < this.options.minChars){
if (this.insufficientInput){ return; }
this.emptyInput = false;
this.insufficientInput = true;
this.emit('insufficientInput', elt);
} else {
this.emptyInput = false;
this.insufficientInput = false;
this.lastQuery = elt.value;
this.emit('search', elt);
}
};
TypeAhead.prototype.onResults = function(elt, results, query){
var triggerNoResults = (!results || !results.length) && (query.indexOf("prefill", 0) == -1);
if (triggerNoResults){
this.emit('noResults', elt);
return;
}
this.emit('results', elt, results, query);
};
return TypeAhead;
});

define('typeahead/query/remote', [
'utils/ajax', 'utils/objutils'
], function(Ajax, Obj) {
'use strict';
var typedSearch = function(types, enableCache, abortRequest) {
return function(options) {
return function() {
var cache = enableCache ? {} : void(0);
var currentXHR;
var addToCache = function(query, response) {
if (cache && response && response.length && response.length > 0) {
cache[query] = response;
}
};
var getFromCache = function(query) {
return cache && cache[query];
};
var getData = function(query, success, error) {
var ops = typeof options == 'function' ? options() : options;
return {
type: 'GET',
url: '/TypeAheadJson',
data: Obj.extend({
action: 'API',
types: types,
filter: 'nobroad',
legacy_format: true,
urlList: false,
strictParent: true,
query: query,
max: 25
}, ops),
dataType: 'json',
xhrFields: {withCredentials: true},
success: success,
error: error
};
};
var abortCurrentRequest = function() {
if (abortRequest &&
currentXHR &&
currentXHR.readyState != 4 &&
typeof currentXHR.abort === 'function') {
try {
currentXHR.abort();
} catch (e) {
}
}
};
this.on('search', function(elt) {
var typeahead = this;
var query = elt.value;
abortCurrentRequest();
var cachedResult = getFromCache(query);
if (cachedResult) {
typeahead.onResults(elt, cachedResult, query);
typeahead.emit('searchResults', cachedResult);
} else {
currentXHR =
Ajax(getData(query,
function(response) {
addToCache(query, response);
typeahead.onResults(elt, response, query);
typeahead.emit('searchResults', response);
},
function(xhr, errorType, error) {
typeahead.emit('error', 'search', errorType, error);
}
)
);
}
});
};
};
};
var Remote = {};
Remote.Geo = typedSearch('geo');
Remote.Geo_Caching = typedSearch('geo', true, true);
Remote.POI = typedSearch('eat,attr,hotel');
Remote.POI_Caching = typedSearch('eat,attr,hotel', true, true);
return Remote;
});

define('typeahead/query/geonavi', ['babel/babel-helpers', 'utils/ajax'], function (babelHelpers, ajax) {
'use strict';
var NAME = 'prefill-geonavi';
var URL = '/TypeAheadJson?action=GEONAVI&geoID=';
var cache = {};
var id = 1;
var stack = [];
return function (options) {
options = babelHelpers['extends']({ limit: 26 }, options);
var _elt = void 0;
return function () {
var _this2 = this;
function geoNavi(elt) {
var _this = this;
_elt = elt;
if (cache[id] instanceof Promise) {
return;
}
var results = this.results ? this.results : [];
if (!cache[id]) {
cache[id] = ajax(URL + id).then(function (res) {
return res.results.map(function (r, i) {
return {
name: r.displayName,
id: r.id,
geonavi: true,
value: r.isLeaf ? r.id : false,
navi: !r.isLeaf,
back: i === 0
};
});
}).then(function (data) {
return cache[id] = data;
}).then(function (data) {
_this.results = [];
_this.emit('emptyInput', elt);
});
results.push({ loading: true, skip: true, selectable: false });
options.header && results.push(options.header);
} else if (cache[id].length) {
options.header && results.push(options.header);
results = [].concat(babelHelpers.toConsumableArray(results), babelHelpers.toConsumableArray(cache[id].slice(0, options.limit)));
}
this.onResults(elt, results, NAME);
};
this.on('emptyInput', geoNavi.bind(this));
this.on('insufficientInput', geoNavi.bind(this));
this.on('selected', function (result, selectionType) {
if (result.geonavi && !result.value) {
if (result.id === id) {
stack.length && (id = stack.pop());
} else {
stack.push(id);
id = result.id;
}
_this2.results = [];
_this2.emit('emptyInput', _elt);
}
});
};
};
});

define('typeahead/support/bindToElement',
['lib/jquery-amd', 'typeahead/TypeAhead'],
function($, TypeAhead){
'use strict';
return function(elmt){
return function(){
var typeahead = this;
var el = $(elmt);
TypeAhead.inputEvents.forEach(function(type){
el.on(type, function(evt){ typeahead.emit(type, evt, elmt); });
}, this);
typeahead.on('show', function() {
if (!typeahead.resultElements) {
return;
}
typeahead.resultElements.map(function(result) {
$(result).on("mousedown", function(evt) {
evt.stopPropagation();
evt.preventDefault();
typeahead.emit('resultClick', evt, this);
});
$(result).on("mouseenter", function(evt) {
typeahead.emit('resultHover', evt, this);
});
$(result).on("mouseleave", function(evt) {
typeahead.emit('resultUnhover', evt, this);
});
$(result).on("touchstart", function(evt) {
typeahead.emit('touchUnfocus', evt, this);
});
});
});
}
};
});

define('typeahead/query/noResults', [], function(){
'use strict';
return function(results){
return function(){
this.on('noResults', function(elt){
this.onResults(elt, typeof results === 'function' ? results(this) : results);
});
};
};
});
define('utils/string', ['utils/errorutils'], function(errorutils){
'use strict';
var RE_TRUE = /^(true|1|on|yes)$/i;
var RE_FALSE = /^(false|0|off|no)$/i;
var utils = {};
utils.fn = function(fn){
switch(typeof(fn))
{
case 'function':
return fn;
case 'string': {
var f = false;
try {
f = eval(fn);
} catch (e) {
errorutils.record(e, "error evaling function");
}
if (!f) {
var ns = fn.split('.'),
n = ns.pop();
try {
ns = eval(ns.join('.'));
f = ns && ns._magic && ns._magic.partial(n);
}
catch (e) {
errorutils.record(e, "function un-parseable");
}
}
if (f && typeof(f) === 'function') {
return f;
}
break;
}
}
return null;
};
utils.parseBoolean = function(str){
return RE_TRUE.test(str);
};
function parseLiteral(s){
if (/^-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?$/.test(s[1])){ return +s[1]; }
else if (/^fn:/.test(s[1])){ return utils.fn(s[1].slice(3)); }
else if (RE_TRUE.test(s[1])){ return true; }
else if (RE_FALSE.test(s[1])){ return false; }
}
utils.parseJSLN = function(str){
return (str || '').split(',').reduce(function(o, v){
var s = v.split(':');
o[s[0].trim()] = parseLiteral(s[1].trim());
}, {});
};
return utils;
});

define('typeahead/ux/selectResult', [
'Logging', 'lib/jquery-amd', 'utils/string'
], function(
Logging, $, Str,
UNDEFINED
){
'use strict';
var SelectResult = function(mode, fn, wrap, selectFirstOnMouseLeave) {
if (arguments.length == 1 && typeof mode == 'string'){
var s = mode.split(',');
mode = SelectResult[s[0]];
fn = SelectResult[s[1]];
wrap = Str.parseBoolean(s[2]);
}
fn || (fn = SelectResult.TOGGLE_CLASS());
return function(){
var selectFirst = function() {
var length = this.results.length;
for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
if (!this.results[i].skip) {
this.selectedIndex = i;
break;
}
}
};
this.on('results', function(elt, results){
this.selectedIndex = -1;
if (!results.length || mode == SelectResult.MODE_NONE){ return; }
if (mode == SelectResult.MODE_AUTO){ selectFirst.call(this); }
else if (mode == SelectResult.MODE_SINGLE){
results.length == 1 && (selectFirst.call(this));
}
else if (mode == SelectResult.MODE_SUFFICIENT){
!this.emptyInput && !this.insufficientInput && elt.value.trim().length && (selectFirst.call(this));
}
this.selectedIndex >= 0 && this.emit('updateSelection', elt, -1);
});
this.on('changeSelection', function(elt, dir){
if (!this.results){ return; }
if (this.selectedIndex === UNDEFINED){ this.selectedIndex = -1; }
var old = this.selectedIndex;
var idx = this.selectedIndex + dir;
while (idx > 0 && idx < this.results.length && this.results[idx].skip){
idx += dir;
}
if (wrap){
if (idx < 0){
idx = this.results.length - 1;
}
if (idx >= this.results.length){
idx = 0;
}
}
idx = Math.min(Math.max(idx, 0), this.results.length - 1);
if (this.selectedIndex == idx){ return; }
if (this.results[idx] && this.results[idx].skip){ return; }
this.selectedIndex = idx;
this.emit('updateSelection', this.resultElements[idx], old);
});
this.on('updateSelection', function(elt, oldIdx, isMouse){
oldIdx >= 0 && fn(this.resultElements[oldIdx], false);
if (!isMouse){
var offsetParent = $(elt).offsetParent()[0];
if (offsetParent){
var offset = $(elt).position();
var edge = $(offsetParent).height();
if (offset.top + elt.offsetHeight > edge){
offsetParent.scrollTop = Math.max(0, offset.top);
} else if (offset.top < 0){
offsetParent.scrollTop = offsetParent.scrollTop + offset.top;
}
}
}
if (!this.results || this.selectedIndex < 0 || this.selectedIndex >= this.results.length){ return; }
if (this.results[this.selectedIndex].selectable === false){ return; }
fn(this.resultElements[this.selectedIndex], true);
});
this.on('enter', function(elt){
if (!this.results || this.selectedIndex < 0 || this.selectedIndex >= this.results.length){ return; }
if (this.results[this.selectedIndex].selectable === false){ return; }
this.emit('selected', this.results[this.selectedIndex], 'enter');
});
this.on('escape', function(elt){
this.selectedIndex = -1;
this.emit('hide');
});
this.on('resultHover', function(evt, choiceElt){
if (!this.results || !this.results[choiceElt.resultIdx] || this.results[choiceElt.resultIdx].skip){ return; }
var idx = this.selectedIndex;
this.selectedIndex = choiceElt.resultIdx;
this.emit('updateSelection', choiceElt, idx, true);
});
if (selectFirstOnMouseLeave) {
this.on('resultUnhover', function (evt, choiceElt) {
if (!this.results) { return; }
var idx = this.selectedIndex;
selectFirst.call(this);
this.emit('updateSelection', choiceElt, idx, true);
});
}
this.on('resultClick', function(evt, choiceElt){
if (!this.results || !this.results[choiceElt.resultIdx] || this.results[choiceElt.resultIdx].skip){ return; }
if (this.results[choiceElt.resultIdx].selectable === false){ return; }
this.emit('selected', this.results[choiceElt.resultIdx], 'click');
});
this.on('selected', function(selection){
this.selectedIndex = -1;
if (!selection.navi) { this.emit('hide'); }
});
this.on('inputChanged', function(elt){
var oldIndex = this.selectedIndex;
this.selectedIndex = -1;
this.emit('updateSelection', elt, oldIndex);
})
};
};
SelectResult.TOGGLE_CLASS = function(cls){
cls || (cls = 'selected');
return function(elt, state){
$(elt).toggleClass(cls, state);
};
};
SelectResult.MODE_NONE = 0;
SelectResult.MODE_AUTO = 1;
SelectResult.MODE_SINGLE = 2;
SelectResult.MODE_SUFFICIENT = 3;
return SelectResult;
});

define('typeahead/options/showResultsOnFocus', [], function() {
'use strict';
return function(){
return function(){
this.on('focus', function(evt, elt){
this.blurTimer && clearTimeout(this.blurTimer);
if (!elt.value){
this.emit('emptyInput', elt);
}
this.emit('show');
});
};
};
});

define('typeahead/options/noInputNoResults', [], function(){
'use strict';
return function(){
return function(){
function clearResults(){
delete this.results;
delete this.resultElements;
delete this.selectedIndex;
this.emit('hideResults');
}
this.on('emptyInput', clearResults);
this.on('insufficientInput', clearResults);
};
};
});

define('typeahead/options/blur', [
], function(
){
'use strict';
var Blur = function(hide, select){
hide = hide !== false;
return function(){
this.on('blur', function(evt, elt){
hide && (this.blurTimer = setTimeout(function(){
this.emit('hide');
}.bind(this), 250));
var queryForResultsSameAsInput = this.results && this.results[0] && this.results[0].query && this.results[0].query === elt.value;
if (
select && this.results &&
this.selectedIndex >= 0 && this.selectedIndex < this.results.length &&
this.results[this.selectedIndex].selectable !== false &&
queryForResultsSameAsInput
){
this.emit('selected', this.results[this.selectedIndex], 'blur');
}
});
};
};
Blur.Select = function(){
return Blur(true, true);
};
return Blur;
});
define('typeahead/support/tracking',
['utils/ajax', 'ta/Core/TA.Record', 'ta/util/Error'],
function (ajax, taRecord, taError) {
'use strict';
var tracking = function (widgetName, searchSessionId) {
var interactionStart = 0;
var createTrackingData = function (eventType, userInteractionType, selectedItem) {
var query = selectedItem && selectedItem.query;
var selectedValue = selectedItem && selectedItem.value;
var selectedUrl = selectedItem && selectedItem.url;
var selectedIndex = selectedItem && selectedItem.resultIdx;
var selectedPlaceType = selectedItem && selectedItem.type;
var selectedDataType = selectedItem && selectedItem.data_type;
var totalCount = selectedItem && selectedItem.totalCount;
return {
action: 'RECORD',
eventType: eventType,
uiOrigin: widgetName,
global: true,
type: selectedPlaceType,
value: selectedValue,
source: widgetName,
startTime: interactionStart,
selDepth: selectedIndex,
isChild: false,
totalNum: totalCount,
userInteractionType: userInteractionType,
errors: null,
scope: 1,
query: query,
dataType: selectedDataType,
url: selectedUrl,
searchSessionId: searchSessionId
};
};
var ajaxTracker = function (trackingData) {
var ajaxParams = {
method: 'GET',
url: '/TypeAheadJson',
data: trackingData
};
ajax(ajaxParams);
};
var mevtCookieTracker = function (trackingData) {
taRecord.addTypeAheadMevt(trackingData);
};
var trackEventViaAjax = function (eventType,
userInteractionType,
selectedItem) {
try {
ajaxTracker(createTrackingData(eventType, userInteractionType, selectedItem));
} catch (e) {
taError.record(e, "typeahead_tracking");
}
};
var trackEventViaMEVTCookie = function (eventType,
userInteractionType,
selectedItem) {
try {
mevtCookieTracker(createTrackingData(eventType, userInteractionType, selectedItem));
} catch (e) {
taError.record(e, "typeahead_tracking");
}
};
var mixin = function () {
var typeahead = this;
typeahead.on('focus', function () {
interactionStart = Date.now();
trackEventViaAjax('start', 'start')
});
typeahead.on('keydown', function() {
if (!interactionStart) {
interactionStart = Date.now();
trackEventViaAjax('start', 'start')
}
});
typeahead.on('selected', function (selection, selectionType) {
trackEventViaAjax('select', selectionType, selection);
});
};
var getInteractionStart = function () {
return interactionStart;
};
var getWidgetName = function () {
return widgetName;
};
var getSearchSessionId = function () {
return searchSessionId;
};
return {
mixin: mixin,
trackEventViaAjax: trackEventViaAjax,
trackEventViaMEVTCookie: trackEventViaMEVTCookie,
getInteractionStart: getInteractionStart,
getWidgetName: getWidgetName,
getSearchSessionId: getSearchSessionId
};
};
return tracking;
});

define('overlays/options/disablePageScroll', ['vanillajs'], function(vanilla) {
'use strict';
return function(){
function disableScroll(){
document.body.style.position = "absolute";
document.body.style.overflow = "hidden";
document.body.style.width = "100%";
}
function enableScroll() {
document.body.style.position = "relative";
document.body.style.overflow = "auto";
document.body.style.width = "auto";
}
this.on('show', disableScroll);
this.on('hide', enableScroll);
};
});

define('utils/geolocation', ['vanillajs'], function() {
'use strict';
var canRequestLocation = function() {
return typeof navigator != 'undefined' && typeof navigator.geolocation != 'undefined';
};
var requestLocation = function(onSuccess, onFailure) {
if (typeof onSuccess !== "function") {
return;
}
if (canRequestLocation()) {
navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
function(response) {
onSuccess({
latitude: response.coords.latitude,
longitude: response.coords.longitude
});
},
function(error) {
if (typeof onFailure === "function") {
onFailure(error);
}
});
} else {
onFailure(new Error("Location services not available"));
}
};
return {
canRequestLocation: canRequestLocation,
requestLocation: requestLocation
};
});require(['ta/prwidgets'], function(widgets) {
var define = widgets.define.bind(widgets,'search_typeahead','handlers',['dt_overlay','handlers']);
/* jshint newcap:false */
define([
  'widget', 'api-mod',
  'lib/jquery-amd', 'utils/ajax', 'common/Radio',
  'dt_overlay',
  'typeahead/TypeAhead', 'typeahead/query/remote', 'typeahead/query/geonavi',
  'typeahead/support/bindToElement',
  'typeahead/query/noResults', 'typeahead/ux/selectResult',
  'typeahead/options/showResultsOnFocus', 'typeahead/options/noInputNoResults', 'typeahead/options/blur',
  'typeahead/support/tracking',
  'ta/util/SessionStorage',
  'ta/util/Error',
  'ta/Core/TA.Record',
  'overlays/Overlay',
  'overlays/styles/modal',
  'overlays/options/repositionOnEvent',
  'overlays/options/disablePageScroll',
  'utils/geolocation',
  "utils/browserutils"
], function(
  widget, api, $, Ajax, Radio,
  TypeaheadUtil,
  TypeAhead, Remote, GeoNavi,
  BindToElement,
  NoResults, SelectResult,
  ShowResultsOnFocus, NoInputNoResults, Blur,
  TypeaheadTracking,
  SessionStorage,
  taError,
  taRecord,
  Overlay,
  Modal,
  RepositionOnEvent,
  DisablePageScroll,
  Geolocation,
  BrowserUtils
){
  'use strict';

  var _widgetDiv = widget.element;
  var _trackContext;
  var selectedResult;

  var maxResults = 6;
  var maxTimeUntilSRPDefault = 2000; // milliseconds (CX-448)

  var $input = $(_widgetDiv).find('.typeahead_input')
  .on('click', function() {
    this.value && this.setSelectionRange(0, this.value.length);
  })
  .one('focus', function() {
    taRecord.trackEventOnPage(_trackContext, 'focus', widgetName);
  });

  // The whole div is clickable, not just the text box inside
  $(_widgetDiv).on('click', function (event) {
    if (event.target === this) {
      $input.focus();
      $input.click();
    }
  });

  var mwInput = api.createElement(
    'input',
    {'type': 'text',
     'class': 'mw_input',
     'placeholder': $input.attr('placeholder'),
     'autocorrect': 'off',
     'spellcheck': 'false'});

  var typesToRequest = $input.data('types') || 'geo';
  var linkType = $input.data('linktype');
  var dataHolder = $(_widgetDiv).find('.data_holder');
  var widgetName = 'trip_search_' + dataHolder.data('widgetname');
  var isAirlinesLander = (widgetName == 'trip_search_Airlines');
  var isMobileWeb = dataHolder.data('ismobileweb') == true;
  var mobileNearbyServlet = dataHolder.data('mobilenearbyservlet');
  var currentLocationLabel;
  var locationDeniedMessage;
  if (!isAirlinesLander && isMobileWeb && Geolocation.canRequestLocation()) {
    currentLocationLabel = dataHolder.data('locationlabel');
    locationDeniedMessage = dataHolder.data('locationdeniedlabel');
  } else {
    currentLocationLabel = '';
    locationDeniedMessage = '';
  }
  var divClasses = dataHolder.data('divclasses');
  var searchSessionId = dataHolder.data('searchsessionid');

  var recentLocationsTitle = dataHolder.data('recenttitle');
  var noResultsMessage = dataHolder.data('noresultsmessage');
  var supportedSearchTypes = dataHolder.data('supportedsearchtypes');
  var recentLocations = [];
  var typeahead;

  var autoPopDatePicker = dataHolder.data("autopopdatepicker") == true;

  var SELECTED_RESULT_KEY = 'selectedTypeAheadResult';
  var previouslySelectedResult = SessionStorage.getObject(SELECTED_RESULT_KEY);

  try {
    var recentLocationsData = dataHolder.data("recentjson");
    if (recentLocationsData.length) {
      if (recentLocationsData.length > maxResults) {
        recentLocations = recentLocationsData.slice(0, maxResults);
      } else {
        recentLocations = recentLocationsData;
      }
    }
  } catch (e) {
    taError.record(e, "typeahead_recent");
  }

  $(_widgetDiv).find('.typeahead_icon').on('click', function(){ $input.focus(); });

  var DefaultResults = function (title, results) {
    return function () {
      var resultsWithTitle = [];
      if (isAirlinesLander && isMobileWeb) {
        resultsWithTitle = [{}]; // since airlines has no nearby location button and default results, an empty list would hide the typeahead
      }
      if (currentLocationLabel) {
        Array.prototype.push.apply(resultsWithTitle, [{name: currentLocationLabel,
        type: 'NEARBY',
        isLatLong: true,
        short: true}]);
      }
      if (title && results && results.length && results.length > 0) {
        Array.prototype.push.apply(resultsWithTitle, [{
          sectionTitle: title,
          skip: true,
          selectable: false
        }]);
        Array.prototype.push.apply(resultsWithTitle, results);
      }

      function Handler(elt) {
        if (resultsWithTitle.length > 0) {
          this.onResults(elt, this.results ? this.results.concat(resultsWithTitle) : resultsWithTitle, '<recently_viewed>');
        } else if (!this.results) {
          this.emit('hide');
        }
      }

      this.on('emptyInput', Handler);
      this.on('insufficientInput', Handler);
    };
  };

  var createMWOverlay = function () {
    var overlay = api.createElement('div', {'class': 'mw_overlay'});
    var inputContainer = api.createElement('div', {'class': 'mw_input_container'});
    inputContainer.appendChild(mwInput);
    overlay.appendChild(inputContainer);
    overlay.appendChild(typeaheadContainer);
    return overlay;
  };

  var overlayContent;
  var typeaheadContainer = api.createElement('div');
  typeaheadContainer.className = 'ui_typeahead_results';

  var classNames;
  if (isMobileWeb) {
    overlayContent = createMWOverlay();
    classNames = 'mw no_padding typeahead_overlay ' + divClasses;
  } else {
    overlayContent = typeaheadContainer;
    classNames = 'dt no_x no_padding typeahead_overlay ' + divClasses;
  }

  var typeaheadTracking = TypeaheadTracking(widgetName, searchSessionId);

  var commonResultsHandler = function(elt, results, query) {
    this.container.innerHTML = '';
    this.results = results;
    this.resultElements = TypeaheadUtil.createResultElements(results, query);
    this.container.appendChild(TypeaheadUtil.listTemplate(this.resultElements));

    // This listener stops results from showing if the user types something then quickly blurs.
    if(elt === document.activeElement) {
      this.emit('show');
    }
  };

  var mwResultsHandler = function (typeaheadContainer) {
    var showSearchOverlay = function(){
      if (!this.searchOverlay) {
        this.searchOverlay = new Overlay(_widgetDiv,
                                        Modal(null, null, classNames, null, null, overlayContent, 'div'),
                                        TypeaheadUtil.mwPosition(),
                                        DisablePageScroll);
      }

      $(mwInput).val('');
      this.searchOverlay.show();
      $(mwInput).focus();
      this.emit('emptyInput', mwInput);
    };

    var hideSearchOverlay = function () {
      this.searchOverlay && this.searchOverlay.hide();
    };

    return function () {

      this.container = typeaheadContainer;

      this.on('results', commonResultsHandler.bind(this));

      // show element containing typeahead results
      this.on('show', function () {
        api.toggleClass(this.container, 'hidden', false);
      });

      // show full-screen mw typeahead overlay
      this.on('showMWOverlay', function () {
        showSearchOverlay.call(this);
      });

      this.on('hide', function () {
        hideSearchOverlay.call(this);
      });
    };
  };

  var dtResultsHandler = function (relativeElement, typeaheadContainer) {
    var showSearchOverlay = function(){
      if (!this.searchOverlay) {
        this.searchOverlay = new Overlay(relativeElement,
                                         Modal(null, null, classNames, null, null, overlayContent, 'div'),
                                         TypeaheadUtil.dtPosition(),
                                         RepositionOnEvent(window, 'resize')
                                        );
      }
      this.searchOverlay.show();
    };

    var hideSearchOverlay = function () {
      this.searchOverlay && this.searchOverlay.hide();
    };

    return function () {

      this.container = typeaheadContainer;

      this.on('results', commonResultsHandler.bind(this));

      this.on('show', function () {
        this.results && this.results.length && showSearchOverlay.call(this);
      });

      this.on('hide', function () {
        hideSearchOverlay.call(this);
      });
    };
  };

  var initTypeAhead = function(inputElement, resultsHandler, selectOnBlur) {

    var addRescueResult = true;
    var typeaheadOptions = {
      searchDelay: 50 // milliseconds (CX-1315)
    };
    if (isAirlinesLander) {
      $.extend(typeaheadOptions, {minChars: 2});
      addRescueResult = false;
    }
    var typeahead = new TypeAhead(
      typeaheadOptions,
      BindToElement(inputElement),
      function(){
        // this has to go here instead of down below because it must come before
        // RecentResults, otherwise the overlay is always closed by the time it
        // sees the event
        this.on('enter', function(elt){
          if (!this.searchOverlay || !this.searchOverlay.isOpen() || this.selectedIndex == -1){
            radio.emit('submit');
          }
        });
      },
      NoInputNoResults(),
      dataHolder.data('geonavi-enabled') ? GeoNavi() : function(){},
      resultsHandler,
      SelectResult(SelectResult.MODE_SUFFICIENT, null, null, true),
      DefaultResults(recentLocationsTitle, recentLocations),
      Remote.POI_Caching(function () {
        return {
          name_depth: 3,
          types: typesToRequest,
          interleaved: true,
          scoreThreshold: 0.5,
          strictAnd: false,
          typeahead1_5: true,
          disableMaxGroupSize: true,
          geoBoostFix: true,
          neighborhood_geos: typesToRequest.indexOf('nbrhd') !== -1,
          details: true,
          legacy_format: true,
          max: maxResults,
          filter: "",
          urlList: true,
          link_type: 'hotel,vr,eat,attr',
          rescue: addRescueResult,
          //tracking
          uiOrigin: typeaheadTracking.getWidgetName(),
          source: typeaheadTracking.getWidgetName(),
          startTime: typeaheadTracking.getInteractionStart(),
          searchSessionId: typeaheadTracking.getSearchSessionId(),
          nearPages: true,
          supportedSearchTypes: supportedSearchTypes
        };
      }),
      ShowResultsOnFocus(),
      NoResults([{
        sectionTitle: noResultsMessage,
        skip: true,
        selectable: false
      }]),
      selectOnBlur ? Blur.Select() : function() {},
      typeaheadTracking.mixin
    )
    .on('focus', function(evt, elt){
      this.emit('emptyInput', elt);
    })
    .on('inputChanged', function(elt){
      selectedResult = null;
    })
    .on('selected', function(selection, selectAction) {
      if (selection.data_type == 'NEAR_POI' && selection.find_near_input) {
        $input.val(selection.find_near_input);
      } else {
        $input.val(selection.name);
      }
      selectedResult = selection;
      if (selection.geonavi && !selection.value){ return; } // handled by geo navi

      $(_widgetDiv).removeClass('error');
      // re-enable the submit button
      radio.emit("disabled", false);
      // if srp typeahead suggesion is clicked, redirect user right away
      if (selection.type && selection.type == 'SEARCH') {
        radio.emit('submit', false);
        SessionStorage.remove(SELECTED_RESULT_KEY);
        $input.val(null);
      } else {
        // Auto execute selection for /R and /A tripsearch, and the typeahead widget used in /Airlines
        if (selectAction === 'click' && (widgetName == 'trip_search_Restaurants' || widgetName == 'trip_search_Attractions' || isAirlinesLander)) {
          radio.emit('submit', true);
        }
        // if user clicks or presses enter to select a typeahead result, then auto pop the date picker
        if ((selectAction === 'click' || selectAction === 'enter') && autoPopDatePicker) {
          $input.blur();
          radio.emit('popDatePicker');
          var checkinInput = api.find('[data-datetype=CHECKIN]');
          if (checkinInput) {
            checkinInput.focus();
          }
        }
        if (selectedResult.type == 'GEO') {
          SessionStorage.setObject(SELECTED_RESULT_KEY, selectedResult);
        }
      }
    })
    .on("touchUnfocus", function() {
      // fix ios browser bug: selecting incorrect result after scrolling overlay
      if (BrowserUtils.Platform.ios) {
        $(mwInput).blur();
      }
    })
    .on('results', function(elt, results, query) {
      if(!$(inputElement).is(':focus')) {
        // CX-448: User must've typed something and then blur'd the field. Select first item from results.
        selectedResult = getFirstValidResult(results, false);
      }
    });
    return typeahead;
  };

  if (isMobileWeb) {
    typeahead = initTypeAhead(mwInput, mwResultsHandler(typeaheadContainer), false);
    $input.on('click', function() {
      typeahead.emit('showMWOverlay');
    });
  } else {
    typeahead = initTypeAhead($input[0], dtResultsHandler(_widgetDiv, typeaheadContainer), true);
  }

  // It's possible to type into the input before this JS and Typeahead JS load, which
  // means we need to signal Typeahead to start a search if $input.val().length > 0.
  // Otherwise we just use the first result in recentLocations if it exists.
  if ($input.val().length) {
    typeahead.emit('search', $input[0]);
  } else {
    var recentLocation;
    if (previouslySelectedResult && !isAirlinesLander) { // We don't want POIs cached for /Airlines
      recentLocation = previouslySelectedResult;
    } else {
      recentLocation = getFirstValidResult(recentLocations, false);
    }
    if (recentLocation) {
      $input.val(recentLocation.name);
      selectedResult = recentLocation;
    }
  }

  var radio = Radio('search')
  .reply('url:require', function() {
    var deferred = $.Deferred();

    if ($input.val().trim().length) {
      typeaheadTracking.trackEventViaMEVTCookie('search', 'click', selectedResult);

      // CX-448: If !selectedResult, give typeahead a little bit more time, but default to SRP if no results.
      if (selectedResult) {
        if (selectedResult.isLatLong) {
          Geolocation.requestLocation(function(coords) {
              selectedResult.latitude = coords.latitude;
              selectedResult.longitude = coords.longitude;
              deferred.resolve(getResultUrl(selectedResult));
            },
            function(error) {
              if (locationDeniedMessage) {
                alert(locationDeniedMessage);
              }
              $(_widgetDiv).addClass('error');
              deferred.resolve(null);
            });
        } else {
          deferred.resolve(getResultUrl(selectedResult));
        }
      } else {
        // If this timer does not get cancelled, we've waited too long and should send user to SRP.
        var timer = setTimeout(function () {
          deferred.resolve(getSRPUrl());
        }, maxTimeUntilSRPDefault);

        var handler = function(elt, results, query) {
          selectedResult = getFirstValidResult(results, false);
          if (selectedResult) {
            // We received results from Typeahead, let's default to the first one.
            deferred.resolve(getResultUrl(selectedResult));
          } else {
            // No results, default to use SRP
            deferred.resolve(getSRPUrl());
          }
          typeahead.off('results', handler);
          clearTimeout(timer);
        };

        typeahead.on('results', handler);
      }
      SessionStorage.remove(SELECTED_RESULT_KEY);
      $input.val(null);
    } else {
      $(_widgetDiv).addClass('error');
      deferred.resolve(null);
    }

    return deferred;

  })
  .on('loading', function(enabled){
    $(widget.element).toggleClass('loading', enabled);
  });

  // Generate search results page URL based off current input value
  function getSRPUrl() {
    return '/Search-q' + encodeURIComponent($input.val());
  }

  function getResultUrl(selectedResult) {
    if (selectedResult.urls && selectedResult.urls.length) {
      var length = selectedResult.urls.length;
        for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
        var url = selectedResult.urls[i];
        if (url.url_type === linkType) {
          return url.url || url.fallback_url;
        }
      }
    } else if (selectedResult.isLatLong) {
      // The selected result is "Current Location"
      if (selectedResult.latitude && selectedResult.longitude) {
        var params = {latitude: selectedResult.latitude,
                      longitude: selectedResult.longitude,
                      sortOrder: 'distLow'};
        if (mobileNearbyServlet === 'MobileNearbyHotels') {
          params.searchFilter = 'hotels';
        } else if (mobileNearbyServlet === 'MobileVacationRentalSearch') {
          //The VR servlet cannot read dates from session => adding dates to the url
          setDates(params);
        }
        return '/' + mobileNearbyServlet + '?' + $.param(params);
      } else {
        return null;
      }
    } else if (selectedResult.geonavi) {
      return '/' + dataHolder.data('widgetname') + '-g' + (selectedResult.value || selectedResult.id);
    }

    // pass search session id into srp for tracking purpose
    if (selectedResult.type == 'SEARCH') {
        params = {
            uiOrigin: typeaheadTracking.getWidgetName(),
            searchSessionId: typeaheadTracking.getSearchSessionId()
        };

        var paramString = $.param(params);
        selectedResult.url = selectedResult.url + '&' + paramString;
    }

    return selectedResult.url;
  }

  function setDates(params) {
    var inDate = getDate('CHECKIN');
    if (inDate && inDate[0]) {
      params.inDay = inDate[0].getDate();
      params.inMonth = inDate[0].getMonth();
      params.inYear = inDate[0].getFullYear();
    }
    var outDate = getDate('CHECKOUT');
    if (outDate && outDate[0]) {
      params.outDay = outDate[0].getDate();
      params.outMonth = outDate[0].getMonth();
      params.outYear = outDate[0].getFullYear();
    }
  }

  function getDate(dateType) {
    if (typeof ta !== 'undefined' &&
      ta.page &&
      ta.page.getDates) {
      return ta.page.getDates(dateType);
    }
    return null;
  }

  function getFirstValidResult(results, typeMustBeGeo) {
    // typeMustBeGeo is used for showing recent results on pageload. We show the parent geo of a hotel, etc. instead of the POI itself.

    if (results && results.length) {
      for (var i = 0; i < results.length; i++) {
        var result = results[i];
        var acceptableGeoType = !typeMustBeGeo || (typeMustBeGeo && result.type && result.type === 'GEO');
        if (result.url &&
          result.name &&
          acceptableGeoType) {
          return result;
        }
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  function _detectContext() {
    var classArray = _widgetDiv.className.toLowerCase()
      .split(' ')
      .filter(function(s) { return s.indexOf('wctx-',0) === 0; });
    if (classArray.length > 0) {
      return classArray[0].substring(5);
    }
  }

  function _init() {
    _trackContext = _detectContext();
  }

  _init();

  return {};
});
});require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'facebook_autologin','handlers',['handlers']);
define([
  'placement', 'lib/jquery-amd', 'ta/Core/TA.Event', 'ta/util/Error',
  'facebook/authutils'
], function(
  placement, $, taEvent, taError,
  fbAuth
){
  'use strict';

  taEvent.queueForAfterLoad(function() {

    var fbAutologinData = $('#fb_autologin_data');
    if (fbAutologinData.length) {
      var loadFbJs = fbAutologinData.data('loadFbJs');
      var facebookJsUrl = fbAutologinData.data('facebookJsUrl');
      var facebookConnectAppId = fbAutologinData.data('facebookConnectAppId');
      var facebookApiVersion = fbAutologinData.data('facebookApiVersion');
      var fbAutoLogin = fbAutologinData.data('fbAutoLogin');
      var fbFetchAccessToken = fbAutologinData.data('fbFetchAccessToken');
    } else {
      taError.record(null, "Could not find Facebook autologin data");
      return;
    }

    try {
      // After the Facebook JS SDK script loads, it should call window.fbAsyncInit
      window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
        fbAuth.init(facebookConnectAppId, facebookApiVersion);
      };

      // If required, load the Facebook SDK asynchronously, as recommended by Facebook
      if (loadFbJs) {
        // Facebook no longer needs an fb-root placeholder element - The Facebook JS SDK creates it on its own, appending it to the BODY tag.
        (function(d, s, id){
          var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
          if (d.getElementById(id)) {
            return;
          }
          js = d.createElement(s);
          js.id = id;
          js.src = facebookJsUrl;
          fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
        }(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));
      }

      // autoLogin returns a promise for the result of the POST back to /FacebookConnectAjax.
      if (fbAutoLogin) {
        fbAuth.queueForInit(function() {
          fbAuth.autoLogin();
        });
      }

      // refreshToken fetches a new Facebook access token from the server.
      if (fbFetchAccessToken) {
        fbAuth.queueForInit(function() {
          fbAuth.refreshToken();
        });
      }
    } catch (e) {
      taError.record(e, "Error setting up Facebook autologin JS");
    }

  }, 'placement: facebook_autologin');
});
});require(['ta/prwidgets'], function(widgets) {
var define = widgets.define.bind(widgets,'homepage_messaging_brand','handlers',['handlers']);
define(["widget", 'lib/jquery-amd', "ta", 'page-model'],
    function (widget, $, ta, pageModel) {

    var pathname = window.location.pathname; //pathname returns "/" for home and "hotels" or "restaurants" etc. for other servlets
    var brandTrackArg;
    var trackedClass = 'tracked';
    var servletName = pageModel.session.pageServlet;

    var trackingTemplate = $(widget.element).find('.brand_pfp').data('trackTemplate');
    if(pathname.length <= 1) {
    brandTrackArg = 'homepage';
    }
    else {
    brandTrackArg = pathname.substring(1).toLowerCase();
    }

    onScroll();

    function track(element) {
    var position = element.getAttribute("data-tpatt");
    var template = element.getAttribute("data-track-template");
    require(["trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record"], function(taRecord) {
        taRecord.trackEventOnPage('Home', 'shelf_click', position + '|brand_messaging|0');
        taRecord.trackEventOnPage('pcb_campaign', 'shelf_click', brandTrackArg + '_brand_shelf' + template + '_click');
    });
    }

    //CRM-6952
    function onScroll(){
      // DOM elements
      var pfp = $(widget.element).find('#middle_column_of_3');
      var featured = $(widget.element).find('#right_column_of_3');

      // Track impressions of visible modules
      if( pfp && !pfp.hasClass(trackedClass)) {
          ta.util.element.trackWhenScrolledIntoView(pfp, ['pcb_campaign', 'scroll', 'PFP_column_inView']);
          addTrackedClass(pfp);
      }
      if (featured && !featured.hasClass(trackedClass)) {
          ta.util.element.trackWhenScrolledIntoView(featured, ['pcb_campaign', 'scroll', 'Featured_column_inView']);
          addTrackedClass(featured);
      }
    }

    var geoId = pageModel.GEO_ID;

    // CRM-7255 - Login Prompt on Brand Shelf - with and without Login Incentive
    var _openViatorRegFlow = function(evt) {
        require('ta/registration/RegOverlay').show(evt, evt.target, {
            flow: 'ATTRACTION_PRODUCT_COMBINED',
            pid: 40102,
            locationId: geoId,
            userRequestedForce: 'true',
            onSuccess: function() {
                _trackAndRefreshPage();
            }
        });
    };

    var _openNonPromoRegFlow = function(evt) {
        require('ta/registration/RegOverlay').show(evt, evt.target, {
            flow: 'BRAND_SIGNUP_CORE_COMBINED', // defined in tr/com/TripResearch/membership/registration/RegistrationFlowId.java
            pid: 40197, // see https://docs.dev.tripadvisor.com/display/CMN/Product+Guide%3A+Registration+and+Login+Tracking
            locationId: geoId,
            userRequestedForce: 'true',
            onSuccess: function() {
                _trackAndRefreshPage();
            }
        });
    };

    function _trackAndRefreshPage() {
        // track.
        // use setEvtCookie as opposed to trackEventOnPage
        // since the page is submitted right away and there is no reason for an additional JSON request
        require(["trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record"], function(taRecord) {
            taRecord.setEvtCookie('pcb_campaign_brandLogin_Success', 'view', 'servletname_'+ servletName, 0, window.location.href);
            // reload the page to ensure the sign up placement is replaced with the regular content in the Brand homepage shelf
            window.location.reload(true);
        });
    }

    function _loginControlClicked(evt, flowName)
    {
        evt.stopPropagation();
        evt.preventDefault();

        require(["trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record"], function(taRecord) {
            taRecord.trackEventOnPage('pcb_campaign_brandLogin_Click', 'click', 'servletname_'+ servletName);
        });

        if (flowName === "viator_registration") {
            _openViatorRegFlow(evt);
        }
        else {
            _openNonPromoRegFlow(evt);
        }
    }

    var $loginButton = $("div.brand_shelf_body.login a");
    $loginButton.on('click', function(evt) {
        // flow name is defined in BrandMessagingModel.java
        var flowName = $("div.brand_shelf_body")[0].getAttribute("data-flow-name");
        _loginControlClicked(evt, flowName);
    });

    // CRM-7407 - Login Prompt on Brand Shelf (#2) - Incentive/non incentive test
    var $rightHandLogin = $("a.inner.right_membership");
    $rightHandLogin.on('click', function(evt) {
        // flow name is defined in BrandMessagingModel.java
        var flowName = $("a.inner.right_membership")[0].getAttribute("data-flow-name");
        _loginControlClicked(evt, flowName);
    });

    // Also, If the sign up version of the widget is displayed, then listen to the regUpdateMember event; it fires upon successfully signing in/up.
    // We need to refresh the page to ensure this placement is replaced
    $(document).on('regUpdateMember', function () {
        if ($loginButton.length > 0 || $rightHandLogin.length > 0) {
            window.location.reload(true);
        }
    });

    // CRM-7521 - Placement on brand messaging shelf for dynamic lander (Desktop)
    var $trackableAnchor = $("a.track_click");
    $trackableAnchor.on('click', function(evt) {
        var property1 = $trackableAnchor[0].getAttribute("data-click-property1");
        var property2 = $trackableAnchor[0].getAttribute("data-click-property2");
        require(["trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record"], function(taRecord) {
            taRecord.trackEventOnPage(property1, property2, 'servletname_'+ servletName);
        });
    });

    // Add a tracked class to the modules so they don't get tracked multiple times
    function addTrackedClass(elem){
      elem.addClass(trackedClass);
    };

    // Event listeners
    $(window).on('scroll resize', function () {
      onScroll();
    });

    return {
    track: track
    };
});});require(['ta/prwidgets'], function(widgets) {
var define = widgets.define.bind(widgets,'shelves_geo_shelf_item_widget','handlers',['handlers']);
define(["widget", "ta/Core/TA.Record"], function(widget, taRecord) {

  // Does element have tracking data 
  function _hasData(element) {
    return element && element.getAttribute && !!element.getAttribute('data-tpp');
  }

  // Get the data
  function _getData(element) {
    if(_hasData(element)) {
      return {
        'property': element.getAttribute('data-tpp'),
        'action': element.getAttribute('data-tpact'),
        'attrib': element.getAttribute('data-tpatt'),
        'pid': element.getAttribute('data-tpid')
      };
    } 
    return null;
  }

  // Shelf Item clicks target same window, so use cookie
  function itemClick(event, element) {
    var data = _getData(element);
    if(data && element.href) {
      taRecord.setEvtCookie(data.property, data.action, data.attrib, data.pid, element.href);
    }
  }

  // CRM-7197 (can be deleted after 11/28/2017)
  function _hasBrandData(element) {
    return element && element.getAttribute && !!element.getAttribute('data-brand');
  }

  function brandClick(event, element) {
    var pathname = window.location.pathname; //pathname returns "/" for home and "hotels" or "restaurants" etc. for other servlets
    var brandTrackArg = (pathname.length <= 1)? 'servletname_Home' : 'servletname_' + pathname.substring(1);

    if (_hasBrandData(element) && element.href){
        taRecord.trackEventOnPage('pcb_campaign_trending', 'shelf_click', brandTrackArg);
    }
  }

  return {
    shelfItemClick: itemClick,
    brandItemClick: brandClick
  };
});
});require(['ta/prwidgets'], function(widgets) {
var define = widgets.define.bind(widgets,'shelves_shelf_widget','handlers',['handlers']);
/*jshint unused:false */
define(["widget", "ta/Core/TA.Event", "lib/jquery-amd", "shelves/ShelfItemPricing"], function(widget, taEvent, $, ShelfItemPricing) {

  var pathname = window.location.pathname; //pathname returns "/" for home and "hotels" or "restaurants" etc. for other servlets
  var brandTrackArg = (pathname === '/') ? 'servletname_Home' : 'servletname_' + pathname.substring(1);

  function shelfSeeAllClick(event, element, sameTab) {
    taEvent.fireEvent('shelf_see_all_click_event', event, element, sameTab);
    event.stopPropagation();
  }

  function trackShelfSeeAllClick(event, element) {
    taEvent.fireEvent('track_shelf_see_all_click_event', event, element);
    event.stopPropagation();
  }

  function leftClick(){
      var shelfWrapper = $('.unscoped_brand_scroll');
      var leftArrow = $('.brand_scroll_arrow.left');
      var rightArrow = $('.brand_scroll_arrow.right');

      leftArrow.hide();
      rightArrow.show();
      shelfWrapper.removeClass('scrolled');

      trackScrollClick();
  }

  function rightClick(){
      var shelfWrapper = $('.unscoped_brand_scroll');
      var leftArrow = $('.brand_scroll_arrow.left');
      var rightArrow = $('.brand_scroll_arrow.right');

      leftArrow.show();
      rightArrow.hide();
      shelfWrapper.addClass('scrolled');

      trackScrollClick();
  }

  function trackFeaturedClick(){
      require(["trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record"], function(taRecord) {
          taRecord.trackEventOnPage('pcb_campaign_trendinglander', 'click', brandTrackArg);
      });
  }

  function trackScrollClick(){
      require(["trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record"], function(taRecord) {
          taRecord.trackEventOnPage('pcb_campaign_trendingscroll', 'click', brandTrackArg);
      });
  }

  // CRM-7197 (can be deleted after 11/28/2017)
  var brandHacItem = $('.shelf_container.popular_destinations')[0];
  var brandTrackedClass = 'tracked';

  function initHAC() {
      var hacList = [];
      var hacMap = {};

      var travelInfo = $('.brand_travel_info');
      var visitDate = travelInfo.data('visitdate');
      var visitLength = travelInfo.data('visitlength');

      if (visitDate && visitLength) {

          $('.poi.brand_hac_item').each(function () {
              var locationId = $(this).data('locationid');
              if (!hacMap[locationId]) {
                  hacList.push(locationId);
                  hacMap[locationId] = true;
              }
          });
      }
      if (hacList.length > 0 && travelInfo) {
          getPrices(hacList, visitDate, visitLength);
      }
  }

  function getPrices(hacList, travelDate, length) {
      var request = new ShelfItemPricing(hacList, travelDate, length);

      request.requestPricings(function(data, seq) {
          var items = data['items'];
          for (var i=0; i<items.length; i++) {
              var priceItem = items[i];
              var locationId = priceItem['location_id'];
              var pricing = priceItem['pricing_string'];
              var status = priceItem['pricing_status'];
              $('.brand_hac_item .hac_' + locationId).each(function() {
                  if (status === 'COMPLETED') {
                      $(this).find('span').html(pricing);
                      $(this).find('.from').show();
                  }
              });
          }
      });
  }

  if (brandHacItem && brandHacItem.getAttribute && brandHacItem.getAttribute('data-brand-shelf') && !brandHacItem.classList.contains(brandTrackedClass) ) {
      brandHacItem.classList.add(brandTrackedClass);
    initHAC();
  }
  return {
    shelfSeeAllClick: shelfSeeAllClick,
    trackShelfSeeAllClick: trackShelfSeeAllClick,
    leftClick: leftClick,
    rightClick: rightClick,
    trackFeaturedClick: trackFeaturedClick
  };
});

define('overlays/options/autosize', ['vanillajs', 'api-mod'], function(vanilla, api) {
'use strict';
return function(padding){
return function(){
var autosize = function (){
var el = api.find('.autosize', this.container);
if (el){
var vH = Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight || 0) - padding;
var oH = api.getSize(this.container).y;
if (oH > vH){
var eH = api.getSize(el).y;
this.container.style.height = vH + 'px';
var h = (eH + vH - oH) + 'px';
var css = document.createElement('style');
css.type = 'text/css';
css.innerHTML = this.container.className
.split(' ')
.map(function(c){ return '.' + c; })
.join('') + ' .autosize { height: ' + h + '; }';
document.head.appendChild(css);
}
}
};
this.on('show', autosize);
};
};

require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'shopping_cart_simple_flyout','handlers',['handlers']);
define(
[
'placement',
'lib/jquery-amd',
'overlays/Overlay',
'overlays/options/autosize',
'overlays/options/autoReposition',
'overlays/options/centerArrowOnSrcElement',
'overlays/options/closeOnChildClick',
'overlays/options/closeOnEscape',
'overlays/position',
'overlays/styles/popover',
'ta/Core/TA.Record'
], 
function(
  placement,
  $,
  Overlay,
  Autosize,
  AutoReposition,
  CenterArrowOnSrcElement,
  CloseOnChildClick,
  CloseOnEscape,
  Position,
  Popover,
  taRecord
) {
  'use strict';

  function SimpleFlyout(targetElement, header, body, cookieId, pageProperty) {
    var overlay = undefined;
  
    function _showAlert() {
    
      if (overlay) {
        return;
      }

      overlay = new Overlay(
        targetElement,
        [
          Popover(targetElement, 'below', '', header.html(), body.html()),
          Autosize(0),
          AutoReposition,
          CloseOnEscape,
          CloseOnChildClick,
          Position.below([8, -20]),
          CenterArrowOnSrcElement(targetElement)
        ]);

      if (overlay) {
        overlay.on('hide', function() {
          taRecord.trackEventOnPage(pageProperty, 'close');
        });

        overlay.show();

        // bounce the cart
        $(targetElement).addClass('animated');

        // request to mark session as seen.
        if (cookieId) {
          $.get('/AttractionCommerceAjax?a=' + cookieId);
        }
      }
    }

    this.show = _showAlert;
  }

  var content = $('.scream_overlay');
  var flyout = new SimpleFlyout($('.shopping-cart-link').get(0), $('.scream_header'), $('.scream_body'), content.attr('data-cookieId'), content.attr('data-pageProperty'));
  $(document).ready(flyout.show);
  return {};
});

});require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'vr_srp_listings','handlers',['handlers']);
define(['placement',
  'lib/jquery-amd',
  'utils/ajax',
  'ta/util/Error',
  'utils/localstorage'
], function (placement,
             $,
             ajax,
             taError,
             localStorage
) {
  var ABANDONED_CART_INFO = "abandonedCart";
  var _placement = $('#' + placement.id);

  var addAbandonedCartCell = function () {
    var abandonedCart = localStorage.get(ABANDONED_CART_INFO);
    if (abandonedCart) {
      ajax({
        url: '/MetaPlacementAjax',
        data:
            {
              /* MetaPlacementAjax parameters */
              placementName: 'vr_abandoned_cart_cell',
              skipLocation: true,
              assets: false,
              packagePrivateAssets: true,
              wrap: true,
              /* AbandonedCartCellRenderer parameters */
              metaReferer: placement.servletName,
              geo: placement.location_id, // UrlArg.LOCATION_ID
              locationId: abandonedCart.locationId, // UrlArg.LOCATIONID
              checkIn: abandonedCart.checkIn, // UrlArg.CHECK_IN
              checkOut: abandonedCart.checkOut, // UrlArg.CHECK_OUT
              inquiryAdults: abandonedCart.inquiryAdults, // VacationRentalsAjax.PARAM_ADULTS
              numOfKids: abandonedCart.numOfKids // VRDetailUtil.PARAM_N_KIDS
            },
        type: 'POST',
        evalScripts: false,
        success: function (data) {
          if (data.indexOf("vr_listing") < 0) {
            return;
          }
          var duplicateListing = $("#vrListing_" + abandonedCart.locationId);
          if (duplicateListing) {
            duplicateListing.closest(".vr_listing").remove();
          }
          _placement.find(".vr_listing:eq(1)").after(data);
        },
        error: function(e) {
          taError.record(e, 'Failed to retrieve abandoned cart cell');
        }
      });
    }
  };

  addAbandonedCartCell();

  return {
  };
